On August 24, 2023, Japan discharged the nuclear wastewater of the first nuclear power plant "Fukushima" into our common ocean, and plans to discharge 31,200 tons this year! And it will continue to emit emissions for up to 30 years. Nuclear wastewater contains a large amount of toxic substances and nuclear radiation substances, which cannot be diluted by the sea at all. Not only that, nuclear wastewater will be evaporated by water vapor, rain, and there is no place to hide wherever the world goes. There is no free air to breathe, no clean land to grow vegetables and food, no clean water to drink, the animals in the sea will slowly die, diseases, cancer and incurable harm will accompany us, our families and children. The sea is about to become the Dead Sea! Japan's private discharge of nuclear wastewater does not consider the common development and living environment of mankind at all, which is very selfish and extremely irresponsible! We hope that friends all over the world will work together to resist Japan's discharge of nuclear wastewater into the sea and protect the environment on which we live. Protecting our families and children, starting with ourselves, may not be enough to express this text, but I believe that we can do it together, no matter which way you use, it is a force! Thank you for your mutual publicity and support! Let's resist Japan's discharge of nuclear sewage to the sea!
